- [ ] 3. Create `src/lib/signals/` directory (if needed) and write `src/lib/signals/diagnosis.ts`.

The V1 source (`C:/users/inteliflow/core/lib/reports/diagnosis.ts`) contains `findRecurringError` as a private function and a richer `diagnoseReport` that covers teacher-report logic. The V2 `diagnosis.ts` lifts only `findRecurringError` verbatim (same body, same filter for `'none'`/`''`) and re-implements `diagnose` for the per-skill/signals context with the spec-specified thresholds (`DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD=25, LOW_HW=50, OK_QUIZ=60, LOW_QUIZ=50`), producing a simpler `{suggestedAction, severity, diagnosis}` shape. `findRecurringError` is now exported for direct use by callers (e.g. the read APIs).

```typescript
// src/lib/signals/diagnosis.ts
// Pure. No imports from next/server, no throws on bad input.
// findRecurringError lifted verbatim from V1 lib/reports/diagnosis.ts:61-74.
// diagnose: signals-layer first-match pattern table (spec §3 diagnosis.ts).

export const RECURRING_ERROR_THRESHOLD = 3;

// Thresholds (spec §3 / Barb-ratified)
const DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD = 25;
const LOW_HW    = 50;
const OK_QUIZ   = 60;
const LOW_QUIZ  = 50;

/**
 * Find the most-frequent non-trivial error_type, or null when nothing
 * recurs >= threshold times. 'none'/'' are filtered out
 * because they aren't real error categories.
 *
 * Verbatim lift of V1 lib/reports/diagnosis.ts:61-74.
 * The caller is responsible for pre-filtering to one skill's error_types.
 */
export function findRecurringError(
  errorTypes: string[],
  threshold: number = RECURRING_ERROR_THRESHOLD,
): { type: string; count: number } | null {
  const counts: Record<string, number> = {};
  for (const e of errorTypes) {
    if (!e || e === 'none') continue;
    counts[e] = (counts[e] || 0) + 1;
  }
  let best: { type: string; count: number } | null = null;
  for (const [type, count] of Object.entries(counts)) {
    if (count >= threshold && (!best || count > best.count)) {
      best = { type, count };
    }
  }
  return best;
}

export interface DiagnoseInput {
  /** Pre-computed divergence score (0–100) */
  divergence_score: number;
  /** Average homework score 0–100; null when no data */
  hw_avg: number | null;
  /** Average quiz score 0–100; null when no data */
  quiz_avg: number | null;
  /** Recent error_type strings for this student+skill (duplicates kept) */
  error_types: string[];
}

export interface DiagnoseResult {
  /** Suggested teacher action */
  suggestedAction: 'reteach' | 'practice' | 'verbal_check' | 'profile';
  /** 1 (mild) to 3 (urgent) */
  severity: 1 | 2 | 3;
  /** Human-readable one-liner for the teacher */
  diagnosis: string;
}

/**
 * Classify one student+skill combination into a suggested action.
 * Returns null when there is nothing actionable (suppress surfacing).
 *
 * Pattern table (first match wins):
 *   1. divergence >= 25 AND hw_avg < 50 AND quiz_avg >= 60 → verbal_check   sev 2
 *   2. divergence >= 25 AND quiz_avg < 50                  → reteach          sev 3
 *   3. divergence >= 25 (generic)                          → profile          sev 1
 *   4. recurring error type                                → practice         sev 2
 *   5. otherwise → null
 */
export function diagnose(input: DiagnoseInput): DiagnoseResult | null {
  const { divergence_score, hw_avg, quiz_avg, error_types } = input;

  // 1. High divergence: doing HW but tanking quizzes (potential copying / coaching)
  if (divergence_score >= DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD && hw_avg != null && hw_avg < LOW_HW && quiz_avg != null && quiz_avg >= OK_QUIZ) {
    return {
      suggestedAction: 'verbal_check',
      severity: 2,
      diagnosis: `HW avg ${Math.round(hw_avg)}% diverges from quiz avg ${Math.round(quiz_avg)}% — consider a verbal check.`,
    };
  }

  // 2. High divergence + low quiz → reteach urgent
  if (divergence_score >= DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD && quiz_avg != null && quiz_avg < LOW_QUIZ) {
    return {
      suggestedAction: 'reteach',
      severity: 3,
      diagnosis: `Quiz avg ${Math.round(quiz_avg)}% with divergence score ${Math.round(divergence_score)} — concept likely needs reteaching.`,
    };
  }

  // 3. High divergence (generic) → flag for closer look
  if (divergence_score >= DIVERGENCE_THRESHOLD) {
    return {
      suggestedAction: 'profile',
      severity: 1,
      diagnosis: `Divergence score ${Math.round(divergence_score)} — check student profile for context.`,
    };
  }

  // 4. Recurring error type → targeted practice
  const recurring = findRecurringError(error_types);
  if (recurring) {
    return {
      suggestedAction: 'practice',
      severity: 2,
      diagnosis: `Recurring "${recurring.type}" errors (×${recurring.count}) — targeted practice recommended.`,
    };
  }

  // 5. Nothing actionable
  return null;
}
```

- [ ] 4. Write `src/lib/signals/conceptGapDetector.ts`.

The V1 source (`C:/users/inteliflow/core/lib/signals/conceptGapDetector.ts`) is a DB-coupled async function that creates its own Supabase client, queries three tables, and calls an OpenAI model. V2 lifts the **constants and gap-detection math** verbatim (`THRESHOLD_PCT=40, MIN_STUDENTS=5`, `pct = Math.round((incorrect/total)*100)`, `pct >= THRESHOLD_PCT`), but makes the function **pure** — the caller provides pre-fetched data. The DB queries and LLM call are caller responsibilities (the read API or cron). This is the one deliberate structural adaptation; all threshold math is verbatim.

```typescript
// src/lib/signals/conceptGapDetector.ts
// Pure. No DB calls, no AI calls, no next/server imports.
// Constants and gap-detection math lifted verbatim from
// V1 lib/signals/conceptGapDetector.ts (THRESHOLD_PCT, MIN_STUDENTS, pct formula).
//
// V2 structural adaptation: pure function over caller-provided data
// (V1 was DB-coupled async; V2 caller fetches data and passes it in).

export const THRESHOLD_PCT = 40; // minimum % incorrect to flag as gap
export const MIN_STUDENTS  = 5;  // need at least 5 attempts per question to detect a pattern

export interface ConceptGapInput {
  questions: {
    questionIndex: number;
    questionText: string;
  }[];
  responses: {
    studentId: string;
    questionIndex: number;
    isCorrect: boolean;
  }[];
}

export interface ConceptGapResult {
  question_index: number;
  question_text: string;
  pct_incorrect: number;
}

/**
 * Detect class-wide concept gaps from pre-fetched quiz response data.
 *
 * A gap is flagged when:
 *   - At least MIN_STUDENTS (5) students answered the question, AND
 *   - At least THRESHOLD_PCT (40)% got it wrong.
 *
 * The threshold math is lifted verbatim from V1:
 *   pct = Math.round((incorrect / total) * 100)
 *   if (pct >= THRESHOLD_PCT) → flag
 *
 * The caller is responsible for generating reteach suggestions (LLM or
 * fallback) and persisting to concept_gaps — kept out of this pure fn.
 */
export function detectConceptGaps(data: ConceptGapInput): ConceptGapResult[] {
  const questionMap = new Map(
    data.questions.map((q) => [q.questionIndex, q.questionText]),
  );

  // Group responses by question index
  const positionStats = new Map<number, { total: number; incorrect: number }>();

  for (const r of data.responses) {
    const stats = positionStats.get(r.questionIndex) ?? { total: 0, incorrect: 0 };
    stats.total++;
    if (!r.isCorrect) stats.incorrect++;
    positionStats.set(r.questionIndex, stats);
  }

  const gaps: ConceptGapResult[] = [];

  for (const [questionIndex, stats] of positionStats) {
    if (stats.total < MIN_STUDENTS) continue;
    // Verbatim from V1: pct = Math.round((incorrect / total) * 100)
    const pct = Math.round((stats.incorrect / stats.total) * 100);
    if (pct >= THRESHOLD_PCT) {
      gaps.push({
        question_index: questionIndex,
        question_text: questionMap.get(questionIndex) ?? `Question ${questionIndex}`,
        pct_incorrect: pct,
      });
    }
  }

  return gaps;
}
```

  ```typescript
  import { describe, it, expect, vi, beforeEach } from 'vitest';
  import { POST } from '../route';
  import { NextRequest } from 'next/server';

  // ── helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  /** Returns the ISO-week Monday (UTC) for the given reference date. */
  function isoWeekMonday(ref: Date): string {
    const d = new Date(Date.UTC(ref.getUTCFullYear(), ref.getUTCMonth(), ref.getUTCDate()));
    const dow = d.getUTCDay(); // 0=Sun … 6=Sat
    const diff = dow === 0 ? -6 : 1 - dow; // Monday offset
    d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + diff);
    return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
  }

  const FIXED_REF = new Date('2026-06-18T00:00:00Z'); // Thursday → Monday = 2026-06-15
  const EXPECTED_MONDAY = '2026-06-15';

  function makeReq(secret: string, refDate?: string) {
    const url = new URL('http://localhost/api/cron/weekly-snapshot');
    if (refDate) url.searchParams.set('ref_date', refDate);
    return new NextRequest(url, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'x-cron-secret': secret },
    });
  }

  // ── mocks ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  vi.mock('@/lib/supabase/server', () => ({
    createAdminSupabaseClient: vi.fn(),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/skills/recomputeSkillStates', () => ({

    computeSessionRisk: vi.fn().mockReturnValue({ score: 0.3, factors: [] }),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/signals/computeEffortLabel', () => ({
    computeEffortLabel: vi.fn().mockReturnValue('independent_success'),

  function makeMockAdmin(opts: {
    activeStudents?: { id: string; school_id: string }[];

    quizResponses?: object[];
    priorSnapshot?: { avg_score: number } | null;
    upsertError?: object | null;
  }) {
    const from = vi.fn((table: string) => {
      const chain: Record<string, unknown> = {};
      const resolve = (data: unknown[], error: unknown = null) => ({
        data,
        error,
        select: () => chain,
        eq: () => chain,
        in: () => chain,
        gte: () => chain,
        lte: () => chain,
        order: () => chain,
        limit: () => chain,
        maybeSingle: async () => ({ data: opts.priorSnapshot ?? null, error: null }),
        upsert: async () => ({ data: null, error: opts.upsertError ?? null }),
      });

      if (table === 'enrollments') {
        return {
          select: () => ({
            eq: () => ({
              data: (opts.activeStudents ?? [{ id: 's1', school_id: 'school1' }]).map(s => ({
                student_id: s.id,
                users: { id: s.id, school_id: s.school_id },
                class_id: 'class1',
              })),
              error: null,
            }),
          }),
        };
      }
      if (table === 'skill_learning_state') {
        return {
          select: () => ({
            eq: () => ({
              data: opts.skillStates ?? [
                { skill: { name: 'Fractions' }, state: 'ready_to_extend' },
                { skill: { name: 'Algebra' }, state: 'needs_more_time' },
              ],
              error: null,
            }),
          }),
        };
      }
      if (table === 'quiz_attempts') {
        return {
          select: () => ({
            eq: () => ({
              order: () => ({
                limit: () => ({
                  data: opts.quizAttempts ?? [{ score_pct: 80, submitted_at: '2026-06-15T10:00:00Z' }],
                  error: null,
                }),
              }),
            }),
          }),
        };
      }
      if (table === 'homework_attempts') {
        return {
          select: () => ({
            eq: () => ({
              order: () => ({
                limit: () => ({

        return {

              data: opts.quizResponses ?? [],
              error: null,
            }),
          }),
        };
      }
      if (table === 'student_model_snapshots') {
        return {
          select: () => ({
            eq: () => ({
              lte: () => ({
                order: () => ({
                  limit: () => ({
                    maybeSingle: async () => ({ data: opts.priorSnapshot ?? null, error: null }),
                  }),
                }),
              }),
            }),
          }),
          upsert: async () => ({ data: null, error: opts.upsertError ?? null }),
        };
      }
      return resolve([]);
    });

    return { from };
  }

  // ── tests ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  describe('POST /api/cron/weekly-snapshot', () => {
    beforeEach(() => {
      vi.stubEnv('CRON_SECRET', 'test-secret');
      vi.mocked(createAdminSupabaseClient).mockReturnValue(makeMockAdmin({}) as ReturnType<typeof createAdminSupabaseClient>);
    });

    it('returns 401 when CRON_SECRET header is missing', async () => {
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/cron/weekly-snapshot', { method: 'POST' });
      const res = await POST(req);
      expect(res.status).toBe(401);
    });

    it('returns 401 when CRON_SECRET header does not match', async () => {
      const res = await POST(makeReq('wrong-secret'));
      expect(res.status).toBe(401);
    });

    it('returns 200 with summary on valid secret', async () => {
      const res = await POST(makeReq('test-secret', '2026-06-18'));
      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
      const body = await res.json();
      expect(body).toMatchObject({ snapshot_date: expect.any(String), processed: expect.any(Number) });
    });

    it('snapshot_date is the ISO-week Monday for the ref_date (deterministic)', async () => {
      const res = await POST(makeReq('test-secret', '2026-06-18')); // Thursday
      const body = await res.json();
      expect(body.snapshot_date).toBe(EXPECTED_MONDAY);
    });

    it('helper isoWeekMonday returns 2026-06-15 for 2026-06-18', () => {
      expect(isoWeekMonday(FIXED_REF)).toBe(EXPECTED_MONDAY);
    });

    it('rolls up strength_topics and struggle_topics correctly', async () => {
      const admin = makeMockAdmin({
        skillStates: [
          { skill: { name: 'Fractions' }, state: 'ready_to_extend' },
          { skill: { name: 'Geometry' }, state: 'on_track' },
          { skill: { name: 'Algebra' }, state: 'needs_more_time' },
          { skill: { name: 'Decimals' }, state: 'needs_different_instruction' },
        ],
      });
      vi.mocked(createAdminSupabaseClient).mockReturnValue(admin as ReturnType<typeof createAdminSupabaseClient>);
      // Verify via upsert call — check what was passed
      let upsertPayload: Record<string, unknown> | null = null;
      admin.from = vi.fn((table: string) => {
        const orig = makeMockAdmin({
          skillStates: [
            { skill: { name: 'Fractions' }, state: 'ready_to_extend' },
            { skill: { name: 'Geometry' }, state: 'on_track' },
            { skill: { name: 'Algebra' }, state: 'needs_more_time' },
            { skill: { name: 'Decimals' }, state: 'needs_different_instruction' },
          ],
        }).from(table);
        if (table === 'student_model_snapshots') {
          return {
            ...orig,
            upsert: async (payload: Record<string, unknown>) => {
              upsertPayload = payload;
              return { data: null, error: null };
            },
          };
        }
        return orig;
      }) as unknown as typeof admin.from;
      vi.mocked(createAdminSupabaseClient).mockReturnValue(admin as ReturnType<typeof createAdminSupabaseClient>);
      await POST(makeReq('test-secret', '2026-06-18'));
      if (upsertPayload) {
        expect((upsertPayload as { strength_topics: string[] }).strength_topics).toContain('Fractions');
        expect((upsertPayload as { strength_topics: string[] }).strength_topics).toContain('Geometry');
        expect((upsertPayload as { struggle_topics: string[] }).struggle_topics).toContain('Algebra');
        expect((upsertPayload as { struggle_topics: string[] }).struggle_topics).toContain('Decimals');
      }
    });

    it('snapshot_schema_version is v2', async () => {
      let upsertPayload: Record<string, unknown> | null = null;
      const admin = makeMockAdmin({});
      admin.from = vi.fn((table: string) => {
        const orig = makeMockAdmin({}).from(table);
        if (table === 'student_model_snapshots') {
          return {
            ...orig,
            upsert: async (payload: Record<string, unknown>) => {
              upsertPayload = payload;
              return { data: null, error: null };
            },
          };
        }
        return orig;
      }) as unknown as typeof admin.from;
      vi.mocked(createAdminSupabaseClient).mockReturnValue(admin as ReturnType<typeof createAdminSupabaseClient>);
      await POST(makeReq('test-secret', '2026-06-18'));
      expect((upsertPayload as { snapshot_schema_version: string } | null)?.snapshot_schema_version).toBe('v2');
    });

    it('improvement_4w is null when no prior snapshot at date-28d', async () => {
      let upsertPayload: Record<string, unknown> | null = null;
      const admin = makeMockAdmin({ priorSnapshot: null });
      admin.from = vi.fn((table: string) => {
        const orig = makeMockAdmin({ priorSnapshot: null }).from(table);
        if (table === 'student_model_snapshots') {
          return {
            ...orig,
            upsert: async (payload: Record<string, unknown>) => {
              upsertPayload = payload;
              return { data: null, error: null };
            },
          };
        }
        return orig;
      }) as unknown as typeof admin.from;
      vi.mocked(createAdminSupabaseClient).mockReturnValue(admin as ReturnType<typeof createAdminSupabaseClient>);
      await POST(makeReq('test-secret', '2026-06-18'));
      expect((upsertPayload as { improvement_4w: unknown } | null)?.improvement_4w).toBeNull();
    });

    it('per-student failure is isolated — other students still processed', async () => {
      const { recomputeSkillStatesForStudent } = await import('@/lib/skills/recomputeSkillStates');
      let callCount = 0;
      vi.mocked(recomputeSkillStatesForStudent).mockImplementation(async (_admin, studentId) => {
        callCount++;
        if (studentId === 's1') throw new Error('simulated recompute failure');
        return { updated: 2 };
      });
      const admin = makeMockAdmin({
        activeStudents: [
          { id: 's1', school_id: 'school1' },
          { id: 's2', school_id: 'school1' },
        ],
      });
      vi.mocked(createAdminSupabaseClient).mockReturnValue(admin as ReturnType<typeof createAdminSupabaseClient>);
      const res = await POST(makeReq('test-secret', '2026-06-18'));
      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
      const body = await res.json();
      expect(body.failed).toBeGreaterThanOrEqual(1);
      expect(body.processed + body.failed).toBe(2);
    });
  });
  ```

- [ ] **Step 2 — Run test (expect FAIL — route is a 501 stub).**


- [ ] **Step 3 — Implement the route.**

  Replace `src/app/api/cron/weekly-snapshot/route.ts` entirely:

  ```typescript
  // src/app/api/cron/weekly-snapshot/route.ts
  // Plan 3 — weekly snapshot cron. Replaces the 501 stub.
  //
  // Trigger: POST /api/cron/weekly-snapshot
  //   Header: x-cron-secret: <CRON_SECRET env>
  //   Query:  ?ref_date=YYYY-MM-DD  (optional; used by tests to pass a fixed date;
  //           defaults to today UTC when absent)
  //
  // Per active student, ORDERED:
  //   1. recomputeSkillStatesForStudent  (fresh per-skill states)
  //   2. roll up strength_topics / struggle_topics from skill_learning_state
  //   3. compute trajectory columns via signals lib
  //   4. UPSERT student_model_snapshots ON CONFLICT(student_id, snapshot_date)
  //      with snapshot_schema_version='v2'
  //
  // snapshot_date = ISO-week Monday (UTC) — deterministic, never wall-clock
  // improvement_4w = avg_score vs snapshot at date-28d; NULL if no prior row
  // Per-student failures isolated + logged; never abort the full job.
  import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
  import { createAdminSupabaseClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';
  import { recomputeSkillStatesForStudent } from '@/lib/skills/recomputeSkillStates';
  import { computeConsistency, computeTrajectory } from '@/lib/signals/consistency';
  import { computeHwQuizDivergence } from '@/lib/signals/computeHwQuizDivergence';
  import { computeRosterRiskIndex } from '@/lib/signals/computeRosterRiskIndex';
  import { computeSessionRisk } from '@/lib/signals/computeSessionRisk';
  import { computeEffortLabel } from '@/lib/signals/computeEffortLabel';

  // ── Helpers ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  /**
   * Returns the ISO-week Monday (UTC) for a given reference date.
   * Deterministic — no Date.now(); callers pass the ref explicitly.
   * ISO week: Monday = 1 … Sunday = 0. Offset: (dow === 0 ? -6 : 1 - dow).
   */
  export function isoWeekMonday(ref: Date): string {
    const d = new Date(Date.UTC(ref.getUTCFullYear(), ref.getUTCMonth(), ref.getUTCDate()));
    const dow = d.getUTCDay(); // 0=Sun … 6=Sat
    const diff = dow === 0 ? -6 : 1 - dow;
    d.setUTCDate(d.getUTCDate() + diff);
    return d.toISOString().slice(0, 10); // YYYY-MM-DD
  }

  // ── Handler ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

  export async function POST(req: NextRequest): Promise<NextResponse> {
    // ── CRON_SECRET gate ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const secret = process.env.CRON_SECRET;
    const provided = req.headers.get('x-cron-secret');
    if (!secret || provided !== secret) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
    }

    // ── snapshot_date: ISO-week Monday (UTC) ───────────────────────────────
    // Accept ?ref_date=YYYY-MM-DD for deterministic tests; fall back to today UTC.
    const refParam = req.nextUrl.searchParams.get('ref_date');
    const refDate = refParam ? new Date(refParam + 'T00:00:00Z') : new Date();
    const snapshotDate = isoWeekMonday(refDate);

    const admin = createAdminSupabaseClient();

    // ── Fetch active students (via active enrollments) ─────────────────────
    const { data: enrollments, error: enrollErr } = await admin
      .from('enrollments')
      .select('student_id, users:student_id(id, school_id), class_id')
      .eq('is_active', true);

    if (enrollErr) {
      console.error('[weekly-snapshot] failed to fetch enrollments:', enrollErr);
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to fetch students' }, { status: 500 });
    }

    // Deduplicate students (a student may be in multiple classes)
    const seen = new Set<string>();
    type StudentRow = { student_id: string; school_id: string; class_id: string };
    const students: StudentRow[] = [];
    for (const row of enrollments ?? []) {
      const sid = row.student_id as string;
      if (!seen.has(sid)) {
        seen.add(sid);
        const u = row.users as { id: string; school_id: string } | null;
        students.push({
          student_id: sid,
          school_id: u?.school_id ?? '',
          class_id: row.class_id as string,
        });
      }
    }

    // ── Per-student processing ─────────────────────────────────────────────
    let processed = 0;
    let failed = 0;
    let skipped = 0;

    for (const { student_id, school_id, class_id } of students) {
      try {
        // ── Step 1: recompute skill states (MUST be first) ─────────────────
        await recomputeSkillStatesForStudent(admin, student_id, { classId: class_id });

        // ── Step 2: roll up strength / struggle from skill_learning_state ──
        const { data: skillStates } = await admin
          .from('skill_learning_state')
          .select('skill:skill_id(name), state')
          .eq('student_id', student_id);

        const strength_topics: string[] = [];
        const struggle_topics: string[] = [];
        for (const row of skillStates ?? []) {
          const name = (row.skill as { name: string } | null)?.name;
          if (!name) continue;
          if (row.state === 'ready_to_extend' || row.state === 'on_track') {
            strength_topics.push(name);
          } else if (row.state === 'needs_more_time' || row.state === 'needs_different_instruction') {
            struggle_topics.push(name);
          }
        }

        // ── Step 3: trajectory columns ────────────────────────────────────

        // Quiz scores (last 20) for consistency + trajectory
        const { data: quizRows } = await admin
          .from('quiz_attempts')
          .select('score_pct, submitted_at')
          .eq('student_id', student_id)
          .order('submitted_at', { ascending: false })
          .limit(20);
        const quizScores = (quizRows ?? [])
          .map((r: { score_pct: number }) => r.score_pct)
          .filter((s): s is number => s != null);

        // avg_score
        const avg_score = quizScores.length
          ? quizScores.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / quizScores.length
          : null;

        // Consistency
        const consistencyResult = computeConsistency(quizScores);
        const consistency_label = consistencyResult.consistency_label;

        // Trajectory (per computeTrajectory from consistency.ts — takes quizScores array)
        const trajectoryResult = computeTrajectory(quizScores);

        // Homework (last 20) for divergence + effort
        const { data: hwRows } = await admin
          .from('homework_attempts')
          .select('score_pct, teli_hint_count, effort_label, submitted_at')
          .eq('student_id', student_id)
          .order('submitted_at', { ascending: false })
          .limit(20);
        const hwScores = (hwRows ?? [])
          .map((r: { score_pct: number | null }) => r.score_pct)
          .filter((s): s is number => s != null);

        // HW/Quiz divergence
        const divergenceResult = computeHwQuizDivergence({
          homeworkScores: (hwRows ?? []).map((r: { score_pct: number | null }) => r.score_pct ?? null),
          quizScores: (quizRows ?? []).map((r: { score_pct: number }) => r.score_pct ?? null),
        });

        // Roster risk (longitudinal 0–100)
        const totalHw = (hwRows ?? []).length;
        const totalQuizzes = (quizRows ?? []).length;
        const completionRate = totalHw + totalQuizzes > 0
          ? totalQuizzes / Math.max(1, totalQuizzes + totalHw * 0.5)
          : null;
        const riskResult = computeRosterRiskIndex({
          avgHwScore: hwScores.length
            ? hwScores.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / hwScores.length
            : null,
          avgQuizScore: avg_score,
          completionRate,
          quizScores,
          hwScores,
        });

        // Session risk — use most recent quiz's responses
        const { data: quizResponses } = await admin
          .from('quiz_responses')
          .select('response_time_ms, hesitation_ms, answer_changes, navigation_backs, pause_count, total_pause_ms, word_count')
          .eq('attempt_id', (quizRows ?? [])[0]?.submitted_at ? (quizRows as Array<{ id?: string }>)[0]?.id ?? '' : '');
        const sessionRiskResult = computeSessionRisk(quizResponses ?? []);

        // dominant_effort_pattern from last 5 homework_attempts.effort_label
        const effortLabels = (hwRows ?? [])
          .slice(0, 5)
          .map((r: { effort_label: string | null }) => r.effort_label)
          .filter((l): l is string => l != null);
        let dominant_effort_pattern: string | null = null;
        if (effortLabels.length > 0) {
          const counts: Record<string, number> = {};
          for (const l of effortLabels) counts[l] = (counts[l] ?? 0) + 1;
          dominant_effort_pattern = Object.entries(counts).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])[0][0];
        }

        // recent_effort_labels — last 5 effort_label values (with score + hint)
        const recent_effort_labels = (hwRows ?? []).slice(0, 5).map((r: {
          score_pct: number | null;
          teli_hint_count: number | null;
          effort_label: string | null;
          submitted_at: string;
        }) => ({
          score: r.score_pct,
          hints: r.teli_hint_count,
          effort_label: r.effort_label ?? computeEffortLabel({ score: r.score_pct, teliHintCount: r.teli_hint_count }),
          submitted_at: r.submitted_at,
        }));

        // avg_hints_per_attempt
        const hintValues = (hwRows ?? [])
          .map((r: { teli_hint_count: number | null }) => r.teli_hint_count)
          .filter((v): v is number => v != null);
        const avg_hints_per_attempt = hintValues.length
          ? hintValues.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / hintValues.length
          : null;

        // improvement_4w — compare avg_score to snapshot at snapshot_date − 28d
        const priorDate = new Date(snapshotDate + 'T00:00:00Z');
        priorDate.setUTCDate(priorDate.getUTCDate() - 28);
        const priorDateStr = priorDate.toISOString().slice(0, 10);
        const { data: priorSnap } = await admin
          .from('student_model_snapshots')
          .select('avg_score')
          .eq('student_id', student_id)
          .lte('snapshot_date', priorDateStr)
          .order('snapshot_date', { ascending: false })
          .limit(1)
          .maybeSingle();
        const improvement_4w =
          priorSnap?.avg_score != null && avg_score != null
            ? Math.round((avg_score - Number(priorSnap.avg_score)) * 10) / 10
            : null;

        // ── Step 4: UPSERT student_model_snapshots ────────────────────────
        const { error: upsertErr } = await admin
          .from('student_model_snapshots')
          .upsert(
            {
              student_id,
              school_id: school_id || null,
              snapshot_date: snapshotDate,
              snapshot_schema_version: 'v2',
              // topic rollup
              strength_topics,
              struggle_topics,
              // scores + counts
              avg_score: avg_score != null ? Math.round(avg_score * 10) / 10 : null,
              total_quizzes: totalQuizzes,
              total_homework: totalHw,
              improvement_4w,
              // trajectory
              consistency_label,
              // risk
              risk_score: riskResult.risk_score,
              // divergence
              divergence_score: divergenceResult.divergence_score,
              divergence_direction: divergenceResult.divergence_direction,
              // effort
              dominant_effort_pattern,
              recent_effort_labels: JSON.stringify(recent_effort_labels),
              avg_hints_per_attempt,
            },
            { onConflict: 'student_id,snapshot_date' },
          );

        if (upsertErr) {
          console.error(`[weekly-snapshot] upsert failed for student ${student_id}:`, upsertErr);
          failed++;
          continue;
        }

        // Suppress unused-var warnings for trajectory + session risk until
        // student_model_snapshots grows those columns in a later migration.
        void trajectoryResult;
        void sessionRiskResult;

        processed++;
      } catch (err) {
        // Per-student failures are ISOLATED — never abort the full job.
        console.error(`[weekly-snapshot] error for student ${student_id}:`, err);
        failed++;
      }
    }

    return NextResponse.json({
      snapshot_date: snapshotDate,
      processed,
      failed,
      skipped,
    });
  }

  // GET stub retained for Vercel cron probe (some environments send GET).
  export async function GET(req: NextRequest): Promise<NextResponse> {
    return POST(req);
  }
  ```

**Interfaces:**

  ```typescript
  import { describe, it, expect } from 'vitest';
  import { CL_VERB_BY_STATE } from '../clVerbs';
  import type { SkillLearningState } from '../clVerbs';

  describe('CL_VERB_BY_STATE', () => {
    it('needs_different_instruction → Reinforce', () => {
      expect(CL_VERB_BY_STATE['needs_different_instruction']).toBe('Reinforce');
    });
    it('needs_more_time → Reinforce', () => {
      expect(CL_VERB_BY_STATE['needs_more_time']).toBe('Reinforce');
    });
    it('on_track → On Track', () => {
      expect(CL_VERB_BY_STATE['on_track']).toBe('On Track');
    });
    it('ready_to_extend → Enrich', () => {
      expect(CL_VERB_BY_STATE['ready_to_extend']).toBe('Enrich');
    });
    it('insufficient_data → null', () => {
      expect(CL_VERB_BY_STATE['insufficient_data']).toBeNull();
    });
    it('not_attempted → null', () => {
      expect(CL_VERB_BY_STATE['not_attempted']).toBeNull();
    });
    it('covers all 6 SkillLearningState values', () => {
      const states: SkillLearningState[] = [
        'needs_different_instruction', 'needs_more_time', 'on_track',
        'ready_to_extend', 'insufficient_data', 'not_attempted',
      ];
      for (const s of states) {
        expect(s in CL_VERB_BY_STATE).toBe(true);
      }
    });
  });
  ```

  Create `src/app/api/teacher/student/[studentId]/signals/__tests__/route.test.ts`:

  ```typescript
  import { describe, it, expect, vi, beforeEach } from 'vitest';
  import { GET } from '../route';
  import { NextRequest } from 'next/server';

  vi.mock('@/lib/supabase/server', () => ({
    createServerSupabaseClient: vi.fn(),
    createAdminSupabaseClient: vi.fn(),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/auth/guards', () => ({
    guardStudentAccess: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue(null),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/utils/scoring', () => ({
    currentMasteryBand: vi.fn().mockReturnValue('grade_level'),
    bandIsVolatile: vi.fn().mockReturnValue(false),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/signals/computeHwQuizDivergence', () => ({
    computeHwQuizDivergence: vi.fn().mockReturnValue({
      divergence_score: 5, divergence_direction: 'aligned',
      divergence_trend: null, hw_avg: 78, quiz_avg: 80,
    }),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/signals/computeRosterRiskIndex', () => ({
    computeRosterRiskIndex: vi.fn().mockReturnValue({ risk_score: 30, risk_level: 'low', risk_factors: [] }),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/signals/computeSessionRisk', () => ({
    computeSessionRisk: vi.fn().mockReturnValue({ score: 0.2, factors: [] }),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/signals/diagnosis', () => ({
    findRecurringError: vi.fn().mockReturnValue(null),
    diagnose: vi.fn().mockReturnValue(null),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/signals/computeReteachEffectiveness', () => ({
    detectCompletedReteachCycles: vi.fn().mockReturnValue([]),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/signals/consistency', () => ({
    computeConsistency: vi.fn().mockReturnValue({ consistency_score: 80, consistency_label: 'consistent' }),
    computeTrajectory: vi.fn().mockReturnValue({ trajectory: 'stable', trajectory_direction: 'flat' }),
  }));

  import { guardStudentAccess } from '@/lib/auth/guards';
  import { createAdminSupabaseClient, createServerSupabaseClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';

  function makeParams(studentId: string) {
    return { params: Promise.resolve({ studentId }) };
  }

  function makeMockAdmin() {
    const from = vi.fn(() => ({
      select: () => ({
        eq: () => ({
          data: [],
          error: null,
          order: () => ({ limit: () => ({ data: [], error: null }) }),
          maybeSingle: async () => ({ data: null, error: null }),
          in: () => ({ data: [], error: null }),
        }),
      }),
    }));
    return { from };
  }

  function makeMockServer() {
    return {
      auth: {
        getUser: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue({ data: { user: { id: 'teacher1' } }, error: null }),
      },
    };
  }

  describe('GET /api/teacher/student/[studentId]/signals', () => {
    beforeEach(() => {
      vi.mocked(createAdminSupabaseClient).mockReturnValue(makeMockAdmin() as ReturnType<typeof createAdminSupabaseClient>);
      vi.mocked(createServerSupabaseClient).mockResolvedValue(makeMockServer() as ReturnType<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof createServerSupabaseClient>>>);
    });

    it('returns 401 when not authenticated', async () => {
      vi.mocked(createServerSupabaseClient).mockResolvedValue({
        auth: { getUser: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue({ data: { user: null }, error: null }) },
      } as ReturnType<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof createServerSupabaseClient>>>);
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/teacher/student/s1/signals');
      const res = await GET(req, makeParams('s1'));
      expect(res.status).toBe(401);
    });

    it('returns guard response when guardStudentAccess rejects', async () => {
      const { NextResponse } = await import('next/server');
      vi.mocked(guardStudentAccess).mockResolvedValueOnce(
        NextResponse.json({ error: 'Forbidden' }, { status: 403 }),
      );
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/teacher/student/s1/signals');
      const res = await GET(req, makeParams('s1'));
      expect(res.status).toBe(403);
    });

    it('returns 200 with bundle on valid auth + guard', async () => {
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/teacher/student/s1/signals');
      const res = await GET(req, makeParams('s1'));
      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
      const body = await res.json();
      expect(body).toHaveProperty('current_band');
      expect(body).toHaveProperty('per_skill_cl');
      expect(body).toHaveProperty('divergence');
      expect(body).toHaveProperty('risk');
      expect(body).toHaveProperty('trajectory');
    });

    it('per_skill_cl uses CL_VERB_BY_STATE — null state → Not yet assessed', async () => {
      const admin = makeMockAdmin();
      admin.from = vi.fn((table: string) => {
        if (table === 'skill_learning_state') {
          return {
            select: () => ({
              eq: () => ({
                data: [
                  { skill: { id: 'skill1', name: 'Fractions' }, state: 'insufficient_data', confidence: 20 },
                  { skill: { id: 'skill2', name: 'Algebra' }, state: 'on_track', confidence: 60 },
                ],
                error: null,
              }),
            }),
          };
        }
        return admin.from(table);
      }) as unknown as typeof admin.from;
      vi.mocked(createAdminSupabaseClient).mockReturnValue(admin as ReturnType<typeof createAdminSupabaseClient>);
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/teacher/student/s1/signals');
      const res = await GET(req, makeParams('s1'));
      const body = await res.json();
      const fractions = (body.per_skill_cl as Array<{ skill_name: string; cl_verb: string | null; cl_display: string }>)
        .find(s => s.skill_name === 'Fractions');
      expect(fractions?.cl_verb).toBeNull();
      expect(fractions?.cl_display).toBe('Not yet assessed');
      const algebra = (body.per_skill_cl as Array<{ skill_name: string; cl_verb: string }>)
        .find(s => s.skill_name === 'Algebra');
      expect(algebra?.cl_verb).toBe('On Track');
    });
  });
  ```

  Create `src/app/api/teacher/class/[classId]/roster-signals/__tests__/route.test.ts`:

  ```typescript
  import { describe, it, expect, vi, beforeEach } from 'vitest';
  import { GET } from '../route';
  import { NextRequest } from 'next/server';

  vi.mock('@/lib/supabase/server', () => ({
    createServerSupabaseClient: vi.fn(),
    createAdminSupabaseClient: vi.fn(),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/auth/guards', () => ({
    guardClassAccess: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue(null),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/utils/scoring', () => ({
    currentMasteryBand: vi.fn().mockReturnValue('grade_level'),
    bandIsVolatile: vi.fn().mockReturnValue(false),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/signals/computeRosterRiskIndex', () => ({
    computeRosterRiskIndex: vi.fn().mockReturnValue({ risk_score: 30, risk_level: 'low', risk_factors: [] }),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/signals/diagnosis', () => ({
    diagnose: vi.fn().mockReturnValue(null),
    findRecurringError: vi.fn().mockReturnValue(null),
  }));
  vi.mock('@/lib/signals/conceptGapDetector', () => ({
    detectConceptGaps: vi.fn().mockReturnValue([]),
  }));

  import { guardClassAccess } from '@/lib/auth/guards';
  import { createAdminSupabaseClient, createServerSupabaseClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';

  function makeParams(classId: string) {
    return { params: Promise.resolve({ classId }) };
  }

  function makeMockServer() {
    return {
      auth: {
        getUser: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue({ data: { user: { id: 'teacher1' } }, error: null }),
      },
    };
  }

  function makeMockAdmin() {
    return {
      from: vi.fn(() => ({
        select: () => ({
          eq: () => ({
            data: [],
            error: null,
            order: () => ({ limit: () => ({ data: [], error: null }) }),
            in: () => ({ data: [], error: null }),
          }),
        }),
      })),
    };
  }

  describe('GET /api/teacher/class/[classId]/roster-signals', () => {
    beforeEach(() => {
      vi.mocked(createAdminSupabaseClient).mockReturnValue(makeMockAdmin() as ReturnType<typeof createAdminSupabaseClient>);
      vi.mocked(createServerSupabaseClient).mockResolvedValue(makeMockServer() as ReturnType<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof createServerSupabaseClient>>>);
    });

    it('returns 401 when not authenticated', async () => {
      vi.mocked(createServerSupabaseClient).mockResolvedValue({
        auth: { getUser: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue({ data: { user: null }, error: null }) },
      } as ReturnType<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof createServerSupabaseClient>>>);
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/teacher/class/c1/roster-signals');
      const res = await GET(req, makeParams('c1'));
      expect(res.status).toBe(401);
    });

    it('returns 403 when guardClassAccess rejects', async () => {
      const { NextResponse } = await import('next/server');
      vi.mocked(guardClassAccess).mockResolvedValueOnce(
        NextResponse.json({ error: 'Forbidden' }, { status: 403 }),
      );
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/teacher/class/c1/roster-signals');
      const res = await GET(req, makeParams('c1'));
      expect(res.status).toBe(403);
    });

    it('returns 200 with roster + concept_gaps on valid access', async () => {
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/teacher/class/c1/roster-signals');
      const res = await GET(req, makeParams('c1'));
      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
      const body = await res.json();
      expect(body).toHaveProperty('roster');
      expect(body).toHaveProperty('concept_gaps');
      expect(Array.isArray(body.roster)).toBe(true);
    });
  });
  ```

  Create `src/app/api/student/growth/__tests__/route.test.ts`:

  ```typescript
  import { describe, it, expect, vi, beforeEach } from 'vitest';
  import { GET } from '../route';
  import { NextRequest } from 'next/server';

  vi.mock('@/lib/supabase/server', () => ({
    createServerSupabaseClient: vi.fn(),
    createAdminSupabaseClient: vi.fn(),
  }));

  import { createAdminSupabaseClient, createServerSupabaseClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';

  function makeMockServer(userId: string | null = 'student1') {
    return {
      auth: {
        getUser: vi.fn().mockResolvedValue({ data: { user: userId ? { id: userId } : null }, error: null }),
      },
    };
  }

  function makeMockAdmin(snapshots: object[] = []) {
    return {
      from: vi.fn((table: string) => {
        if (table === 'student_model_snapshots') {
          return {
            select: () => ({
              eq: () => ({
                order: () => ({
                  limit: () => ({
                    data: snapshots,
                    error: null,
                  }),
                }),
              }),
            }),
          };
        }
        // Ensure skill_learning_state is NEVER queried from this route
        if (table === 'skill_learning_state') {
          throw new Error('student/growth MUST NOT query skill_learning_state');
        }
        return { select: () => ({ eq: () => ({ data: [], error: null }) }) };
      }),
    };
  }

  describe('GET /api/student/growth', () => {
    beforeEach(() => {
      vi.mocked(createServerSupabaseClient).mockResolvedValue(makeMockServer() as ReturnType<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof createServerSupabaseClient>>>);
      vi.mocked(createAdminSupabaseClient).mockReturnValue(makeMockAdmin() as ReturnType<typeof createAdminSupabaseClient>);
    });

    it('returns 401 when not authenticated', async () => {
      vi.mocked(createServerSupabaseClient).mockResolvedValue(makeMockServer(null) as ReturnType<Awaited<ReturnType<typeof createServerSupabaseClient>>>);
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/student/growth');
      const res = await GET(req);
      expect(res.status).toBe(401);
    });

    it('returns cold-start response when no snapshots exist', async () => {
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/student/growth');
      const res = await GET(req);
      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
      const body = await res.json();
      expect(body.cold_start).toBe(true);
      expect(body).toHaveProperty('message');
    });

    it('returns snapshot-based growth when snapshots exist', async () => {
      vi.mocked(createAdminSupabaseClient).mockReturnValue(makeMockAdmin([
        {
          snapshot_date: '2026-06-15',
          avg_score: 80,
          mastery_band: 'grade_level',
          consistency_label: 'consistent',
          dominant_effort_pattern: 'independent_success',
          strength_topics: ['Fractions'],
          struggle_topics: ['Algebra'],
          improvement_4w: 5,
          snapshot_schema_version: 'v2',
        },
        {
          snapshot_date: '2026-06-08',
          avg_score: 75,
          mastery_band: 'grade_level',
          consistency_label: 'variable',
          dominant_effort_pattern: null,
          strength_topics: [],
          struggle_topics: ['Algebra'],
          improvement_4w: null,
          snapshot_schema_version: 'v2',
        },
      ]) as ReturnType<typeof createAdminSupabaseClient>);
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/student/growth');
      const res = await GET(req);
      expect(res.status).toBe(200);
      const body = await res.json();
      expect(body.cold_start).toBe(false);
      expect(body.snapshots.length).toBeGreaterThan(0);
      expect(body.snapshots[0]).toHaveProperty('snapshot_date');
      expect(body.snapshots[0]).toHaveProperty('avg_score');
    });

    it('NEVER queries skill_learning_state (RLS constraint)', async () => {
      // The mock throws if skill_learning_state is accessed
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/student/growth');
      await expect(GET(req)).resolves.not.toThrow();
    });

    it('improvement_4w null on first snapshot (cold-start improvement)', async () => {
      vi.mocked(createAdminSupabaseClient).mockReturnValue(makeMockAdmin([
        {
          snapshot_date: '2026-06-15',
          avg_score: 72,
          mastery_band: 'grade_level',
          consistency_label: null,
          dominant_effort_pattern: null,
          strength_topics: [],
          struggle_topics: [],
          improvement_4w: null,
          snapshot_schema_version: 'v2',
        },
      ]) as ReturnType<typeof createAdminSupabaseClient>);
      const req = new NextRequest('http://localhost/api/student/growth');
      const res = await GET(req);
      const body = await res.json();
      expect(body.cold_start).toBe(false);
      expect(body.snapshots[0].improvement_4w).toBeNull();
    });
  });
  ```

- [ ] **Step 3a — Create `src/lib/skills/clVerbs.ts`.**

  ```typescript
  // src/lib/skills/clVerbs.ts
  // CL verb display layer over the 6 skill_learning_state values (spec §3.2).
  // Moved here from src/lib/auth/roles.ts (cleaner home — skills lib, not auth).
  //
  // null = cold-start "Not yet assessed" (never a fabricated verb).
  // DB enum is internal-only; the teacher never sees the raw state.

  export type SkillLearningState =
    | 'needs_different_instruction'
    | 'needs_more_time'
    | 'on_track'
    | 'ready_to_extend'
    | 'insufficient_data'
    | 'not_attempted';

  /** Map skill_learning_state → CL verb shown in teacher UI.
   *  null means cold-start → render "Not yet assessed". */
  export const CL_VERB_BY_STATE: Record<SkillLearningState, 'Reinforce' | 'On Track' | 'Enrich' | null> = {
    needs_different_instruction: 'Reinforce',
    needs_more_time: 'Reinforce',
    on_track: 'On Track',
    ready_to_extend: 'Enrich',
    insufficient_data: null,
    not_attempted: null,
  } as const;
  ```

- [ ] **Step 3b — Update `src/lib/auth/roles.ts` — remove CL_VERB_BY_STATE, keep rest.**

  Current content of `src/lib/auth/roles.ts`:

  ```typescript
  // Canonical role model (spec §1.2). The DB CHECK in migration 0001 carries the
  // same 6 values; this is the code-side mirror. `school_sysadmin` is the 6th role
  // V1 code depends on but the V1 000 enum omitted — reconciled here + in 0001.
  export const ROLES = [
    'teacher', 'student', 'parent', 'school_admin', 'school_sysadmin', 'platform_admin',
  ] as const;
  export type Role = (typeof ROLES)[number];

  /** Roles routed through the School Admin route group + passing guardSchoolAdmin. */
  export const SCHOOL_ADMIN_ROLES = ['school_admin', 'school_sysadmin', 'platform_admin'] as const;

  /** CL verb display layer over the 6 skill_learning_state values (spec §3.2).
   *  null = cold-start "Not yet assessed" (never a fabricated verb). DB enum is
   *  internal-only; the teacher never sees the raw state. */
  export const CL_VERB_BY_STATE = {
    needs_different_instruction: 'Reinforce',
    needs_more_time: 'Reinforce',
    on_track: 'On Track',
    ready_to_extend: 'Enrich',
    insufficient_data: null,
    not_attempted: null,
  } as const;
  ```

  Replace with (remove CL_VERB_BY_STATE block; add re-export for backward compat):

  ```typescript
  // Canonical role model (spec §1.2). The DB CHECK in migration 0001 carries the
  // same 6 values; this is the code-side mirror. `school_sysadmin` is the 6th role
  // V1 code depends on but the V1 000 enum omitted — reconciled here + in 0001.
  export const ROLES = [
    'teacher', 'student', 'parent', 'school_admin', 'school_sysadmin', 'platform_admin',
  ] as const;
  export type Role = (typeof ROLES)[number];

  /** Roles routed through the School Admin route group + passing guardSchoolAdmin. */
  export const SCHOOL_ADMIN_ROLES = ['school_admin', 'school_sysadmin', 'platform_admin'] as const;

  // CL_VERB_BY_STATE moved to src/lib/skills/clVerbs.ts (Plan 3).
  // Re-exported here for backward compatibility with any existing importers.
  export { CL_VERB_BY_STATE } from '@/lib/skills/clVerbs';
  ```

- [ ] **Step 3c — Create `src/app/api/teacher/student/[studentId]/signals/route.ts`.**

  ```typescript
  // src/app/api/teacher/student/[studentId]/signals/route.ts
  // GET /api/teacher/student/[studentId]/signals
  //
  // One-student signal bundle for the teacher view (Plan 3 read API).
  // Auth: auth.getUser() → 401.
  // Guard: guardStudentAccess(studentId) → 403.
  // Returns: current_band, per_skill_cl (CL_VERB_BY_STATE; null → "Not yet assessed"),
  //          recurring misconceptions per skill, divergence, effort pattern,
  //          both risk reads, reteach outcomes, trajectory.
  // Pure aggregation over lib + tables — no signal math inline.
  import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
  import { createServerSupabaseClient, createAdminSupabaseClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';
  import { guardStudentAccess } from '@/lib/auth/guards';
  import { CL_VERB_BY_STATE } from '@/lib/skills/clVerbs';
  import type { SkillLearningState } from '@/lib/skills/clVerbs';
  import { currentMasteryBand } from '@/lib/utils/scoring';
  import { computeHwQuizDivergence } from '@/lib/signals/computeHwQuizDivergence';
  import { computeRosterRiskIndex } from '@/lib/signals/computeRosterRiskIndex';
  import { computeSessionRisk } from '@/lib/signals/computeSessionRisk';
  import { findRecurringError } from '@/lib/signals/diagnosis';
  import { detectCompletedReteachCycles } from '@/lib/signals/computeReteachEffectiveness';
  import { computeConsistency, computeTrajectory } from '@/lib/signals/consistency';

  // Confidence score → soft human-readable label (teacher-facing; no hard numbers).
  function confidenceSoftLabel(confidence: number | null): string {
    if (confidence == null) return 'unknown';
    if (confidence >= 70) return 'high';
    if (confidence >= 40) return 'moderate';
    return 'low';
  }

  export async function GET(
    _req: NextRequest,
    { params }: { params: Promise<{ studentId: string }> },
  ): Promise<NextResponse> {
    // ── Auth ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const supabase = await createServerSupabaseClient();
    const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (authError || !user) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
    }

    const { studentId } = await params;

    // ── Object-level guard ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const guard = await guardStudentAccess(studentId);
    if (guard) return guard;

    const admin = createAdminSupabaseClient();

    // ── Quiz attempts → current band ───────────────────────────────────────
    const { data: quizAttempts } = await admin
      .from('quiz_attempts')
      .select('mastery_band, submitted_at, created_at, is_complete, score_pct')
      .eq('student_id', studentId)
      .order('submitted_at', { ascending: false })
      .limit(20);

    const current_band = currentMasteryBand(quizAttempts ?? []);
    const quizScores = (quizAttempts ?? [])
      .map((r: { score_pct: number }) => r.score_pct)
      .filter((s): s is number => s != null);

    // ── Per-skill CL ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const { data: skillStates } = await admin
      .from('skill_learning_state')
      .select('skill:skill_id(id, name), state, confidence')
      .eq('student_id', studentId);

    const per_skill_cl = (skillStates ?? []).map((row: {
      skill: { id: string; name: string } | null;
      state: string;
      confidence: number | null;
    }) => {
      const state = row.state as SkillLearningState;
      const cl_verb = CL_VERB_BY_STATE[state] ?? null;
      return {
        skill_id: row.skill?.id ?? null,
        skill_name: row.skill?.name ?? 'Unknown',
        state,
        cl_verb,
        cl_display: cl_verb ?? 'Not yet assessed',
        confidence_label: confidenceSoftLabel(row.confidence),
      };
    });

    // ── Recurring misconceptions per skill ─────────────────────────────────
    const { data: misconceptions } = await admin
      .from('misconception_observations')
      .select('skill_id, error_type, reasoning_pattern, observed_at')
      .eq('student_id', studentId);

    // Group by skill_id
    const bySkill: Record<string, string[]> = {};
    for (const m of misconceptions ?? []) {
      const sid = m.skill_id as string;
      if (!bySkill[sid]) bySkill[sid] = [];
      bySkill[sid].push(m.error_type as string);
    }
    const recurring_misconceptions = Object.entries(bySkill).map(([skill_id, errorTypes]) => ({
      skill_id,
      recurring_error: findRecurringError(errorTypes),
    })).filter(r => r.recurring_error != null);

    // ── Homework attempts ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const { data: hwAttempts } = await admin
      .from('homework_attempts')
      .select('score_pct, teli_hint_count, effort_label, submitted_at, allow_redo, is_redo, id')
      .eq('student_id', studentId)
      .order('submitted_at', { ascending: false })
      .limit(20);

    const hwScores = (hwAttempts ?? [])
      .map((r: { score_pct: number | null }) => r.score_pct)
      .filter((s): s is number => s != null);

    // ── Divergence ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const divergence = computeHwQuizDivergence({
      homeworkScores: (hwAttempts ?? []).map((r: { score_pct: number | null }) => r.score_pct ?? null),
      quizScores: (quizAttempts ?? []).map((r: { score_pct: number }) => r.score_pct ?? null),
    });

    // ── Effort pattern (dominant from last 5 hw effort_labels) ────────────
    const effortLabels = (hwAttempts ?? [])
      .slice(0, 5)
      .map((r: { effort_label: string | null }) => r.effort_label)
      .filter((l): l is string => l != null);
    let dominant_effort_pattern: string | null = null;
    if (effortLabels.length > 0) {
      const counts: Record<string, number> = {};
      for (const l of effortLabels) counts[l] = (counts[l] ?? 0) + 1;
      dominant_effort_pattern = Object.entries(counts).sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])[0][0];
    }

    // ── Risk (both reads) ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const completionRate = quizScores.length + hwScores.length > 0
      ? quizScores.length / Math.max(1, quizScores.length + hwScores.length * 0.5)
      : null;
    const roster_risk = computeRosterRiskIndex({
      avgHwScore: hwScores.length ? hwScores.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / hwScores.length : null,
      avgQuizScore: quizScores.length ? quizScores.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / quizScores.length : null,
      completionRate,
      quizScores,
      hwScores,
    });

    // Session risk from most-recent quiz's responses
    const latestAttemptId = (quizAttempts as Array<{ id?: string }>)?.[0]?.id ?? '';
    const { data: quizResponses } = await admin
      .from('quiz_responses')
      .select('response_time_ms, hesitation_ms, answer_changes, navigation_backs, pause_count, total_pause_ms, word_count')
      .eq('attempt_id', latestAttemptId);
    const session_risk = computeSessionRisk(quizResponses ?? []);

    // ── Reteach outcomes ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const reteach_outcomes = detectCompletedReteachCycles(hwAttempts ?? [], new Set());

    // ── Trajectory (consistency + trend) ──────────────────────────────────
    const consistency = computeConsistency(quizScores);
    const trajectoryResult = computeTrajectory(quizScores);

    return NextResponse.json({
      student_id: studentId,
      current_band,
      per_skill_cl,
      recurring_misconceptions,
      divergence,
      effort: { dominant_effort_pattern },
      risk: {
        roster: roster_risk,
        session: session_risk,
      },
      reteach_outcomes,
      trajectory: {
        ...consistency,
        ...trajectoryResult,
      },
    });
  }
  ```

- [ ] **Step 3d — Create `src/app/api/teacher/class/[classId]/roster-signals/route.ts`.**

  ```typescript
  // src/app/api/teacher/class/[classId]/roster-signals/route.ts
  // GET /api/teacher/class/[classId]/roster-signals
  //
  // Roster-level signal bundle for the teacher view.
  // Auth: auth.getUser() → 401.
  // Guard: guardClassAccess(classId) → 403.
  // Returns: per-student (band + volatility + risk), diagnose-driven focus group,
  //          class-wide concept gaps.
  import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
  import { createServerSupabaseClient, createAdminSupabaseClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';
  import { guardClassAccess } from '@/lib/auth/guards';
  import { currentMasteryBand, bandIsVolatile } from '@/lib/utils/scoring';
  import { computeRosterRiskIndex } from '@/lib/signals/computeRosterRiskIndex';
  import { diagnose } from '@/lib/signals/diagnosis';
  import { detectConceptGaps } from '@/lib/signals/conceptGapDetector';

  export async function GET(
    _req: NextRequest,
    { params }: { params: Promise<{ classId: string }> },
  ): Promise<NextResponse> {
    // ── Auth ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const supabase = await createServerSupabaseClient();
    const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (authError || !user) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
    }

    const { classId } = await params;

    // ── Object-level guard ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const guard = await guardClassAccess(classId);
    if (guard) return guard;

    const admin = createAdminSupabaseClient();

    // ── Enrolled students ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const { data: enrollments } = await admin
      .from('enrollments')
      .select('student_id, users:student_id(id, full_name)')
      .eq('class_id', classId)
      .eq('is_active', true);

    const students = (enrollments ?? []).map((e: {
      student_id: string;
      users: { id: string; full_name: string } | null;
    }) => ({
      student_id: e.student_id,
      full_name: e.users?.full_name ?? 'Student',
    }));

    // ── Per-student signals ────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const roster = await Promise.all(
      students.map(async ({ student_id, full_name }) => {
        const { data: quizAttempts } = await admin
          .from('quiz_attempts')
          .select('mastery_band, submitted_at, created_at, is_complete, score_pct')
          .eq('student_id', student_id)
          .order('submitted_at', { ascending: false })
          .limit(10);

        const { data: hwAttempts } = await admin
          .from('homework_attempts')
          .select('score_pct, teli_hint_count')
          .eq('student_id', student_id)
          .order('submitted_at', { ascending: false })
          .limit(10);

        const quizScores = (quizAttempts ?? [])
          .map((r: { score_pct: number }) => r.score_pct)
          .filter((s): s is number => s != null);
        const hwScores = (hwAttempts ?? [])
          .map((r: { score_pct: number | null }) => r.score_pct)
          .filter((s): s is number => s != null);

        const band = currentMasteryBand(quizAttempts ?? []);
        const volatile = bandIsVolatile(quizAttempts ?? []);

        const hwAvg = hwScores.length ? hwScores.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / hwScores.length : null;
        const quizAvg = quizScores.length ? quizScores.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / quizScores.length : null;
        const completionRate = quizScores.length + hwScores.length > 0
          ? quizScores.length / Math.max(1, quizScores.length + hwScores.length * 0.5)
          : null;

        const risk = computeRosterRiskIndex({
          avgHwScore: hwAvg,
          avgQuizScore: quizAvg,
          completionRate,
          quizScores,
          hwScores,
        });

        const avgHintsArr = (hwAttempts ?? []).map((r: { teli_hint_count: number | null }) => r.teli_hint_count ?? 0);
        const avgHints = avgHintsArr.length
          ? avgHintsArr.reduce((a: number, b: number) => a + b, 0) / avgHintsArr.length
          : null;

        // diagnose — returns null when no concerns
        const diagnosis = diagnose({
          hwAvg,
          quizAvg,
          divergencePts: hwAvg != null && quizAvg != null ? Math.abs(hwAvg - quizAvg) : 0,
          avgHints,
          errorTypes: [],
        });

        return {
          student_id,
          full_name,
          band,
          volatile,
          risk,
          diagnosis,
        };
      }),
    );

    // ── Focus group (students where diagnosis is not null) ─────────────────
    const focus_group = roster
      .filter(r => r.diagnosis != null)
      .map(r => ({ student_id: r.student_id, full_name: r.full_name, diagnosis: r.diagnosis }));

    // ── Class-wide concept gaps ────────────────────────────────────────────
    // Collect misconception observations for all students in this class
    const studentIds = students.map(s => s.student_id);
    const { data: misconceptions } = await admin
      .from('misconception_observations')
      .select('student_id, skill_id, error_type')
      .in('student_id', studentIds.length > 0 ? studentIds : ['__none__']);

    const concept_gaps = detectConceptGaps({
      observations: (misconceptions ?? []).map((m: {
        student_id: string;
        skill_id: string;
        error_type: string;
      }) => m),
      totalStudents: students.length,
    });

    return NextResponse.json({
      class_id: classId,
      roster: roster.map(r => ({
        student_id: r.student_id,
        full_name: r.full_name,
        band: r.band,
        volatile: r.volatile,
        risk: r.risk,
      })),
      focus_group,
      concept_gaps,
    });
  }
  ```

- [ ] **Step 3e — Create `src/app/api/student/growth/route.ts`.**

  ```typescript
  // src/app/api/student/growth/route.ts
  // GET /api/student/growth
  //
  // Student-facing growth view. Reads ONLY student_model_snapshots.
  // NEVER reads skill_learning_state (students cannot read it per RLS —
  // this route enforces that at the code level too).
  //
  // Auth: auth.getUser() → student reads own snapshots.
  // Cold-start friendly: no snapshots → { cold_start: true, message }.
  import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
  import { createServerSupabaseClient, createAdminSupabaseClient } from '@/lib/supabase/server';

  export async function GET(_req: NextRequest): Promise<NextResponse> {
    // ── Auth ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    const supabase = await createServerSupabaseClient();
    const { data: { user }, error: authError } = await supabase.auth.getUser();
    if (authError || !user) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Unauthorized' }, { status: 401 });
    }

    const admin = createAdminSupabaseClient();

    // ── Read snapshots — student reads ONLY their own rows ─────────────────
    // Note: RLS on student_model_snapshots already enforces student_id = auth.uid()
    // for authenticated role, but we bind the student_id filter explicitly here
    // so this route is safe even if called with a service-role client in tests.
    const { data: snapshots, error: snapErr } = await admin
      .from('student_model_snapshots')
      .select(
        'snapshot_date, avg_score, mastery_band, consistency_label, dominant_effort_pattern, strength_topics, struggle_topics, improvement_4w, snapshot_schema_version',
      )
      .eq('student_id', user.id)
      .order('snapshot_date', { ascending: false })
      .limit(12); // ~3 months of weekly snapshots

    if (snapErr) {
      console.error('[student/growth] snapshots fetch error:', snapErr);
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Failed to fetch growth data' }, { status: 500 });
    }

    // ── Cold-start: no snapshots yet ───────────────────────────────────────
    if (!snapshots || snapshots.length === 0) {
      return NextResponse.json({
        cold_start: true,
        message: 'Just getting started — check back after your first few quizzes to see your growth.',
        snapshots: [],
      });
    }

    // ── Return snapshot-framed growth view ─────────────────────────────────
    // Shape is intentionally student-facing: no internal state names exposed.
    const formattedSnapshots = snapshots.map((s: {
      snapshot_date: string;
      avg_score: number | null;
      mastery_band: string | null;
      consistency_label: string | null;
      dominant_effort_pattern: string | null;
      strength_topics: string[] | null;
      struggle_topics: string[] | null;
      improvement_4w: number | null;
      snapshot_schema_version: string | null;
    }) => ({
      snapshot_date: s.snapshot_date,
      avg_score: s.avg_score,
      mastery_band: s.mastery_band,
      consistency_label: s.consistency_label,
      dominant_effort_pattern: s.dominant_effort_pattern,
      strength_topics: s.strength_topics ?? [],
      struggle_topics: s.struggle_topics ?? [],
      improvement_4w: s.improvement_4w,
    }));

    return NextResponse.json({
      cold_start: false,
      snapshots: formattedSnapshots,
    });
  }
  ```
