## ⚠️ Review Corrections (apply per cited task — from controller assembly self-review)

> The task slices were authored in parallel; these corrections resolve cross-slice issues the authors could not see. **Apply each before executing its task; it GOVERNS over the task body where they conflict.** Schema facts verified against `supabase/migrations/*` on 2026-06-18.

- **P3-C1 — `school_id` does NOT come from `lessons` (Task 4).** The `lessons` table has **no `school_id` column** (verified: `0003_lessons_quizzes.sql`). The quiz-gen route's `resolveSkillIds` call needs `schoolId` — derive it from the **class** (`quizzes.class_id → classes.school_id`) or the authed teacher (`users.school_id` for `user.id`). The route already loads the class for `guardClassAccess`; reuse that `school_id`. Do NOT add `lessons.school_id` to the select (it will error). `resolveSkillIds`' `schoolId` arg is then a real non-null uuid.

- **P3-C2 — `misconception_observations.quiz_response_id` must be the real `quiz_responses.id` uuid, not a composite string (Task 13).** `quiz_responses` HAS an `id uuid PRIMARY KEY` (verified: `0003`). The FK `quiz_response_id REFERENCES quiz_responses(id)` requires that uuid. The submit route must obtain each graded response's real `id` (select it back, or capture it from the upsert/update `.select('id')`) and pass it to `recordMisconceptions` — do NOT use `"${attemptId}:${position}"`. If obtaining the id is impractical inline, make `quiz_response_id` nullable in `0011` and still write the row keyed by `(student_id, skill_id, error_type)` — but the uuid is strongly preferred. (Adjust the `0011` FK accordingly if nullable.)

- **P3-C3 — Session risk + trajectory are READ-API-LIVE, not snapshot columns (Tasks 15, 16).** `student_model_snapshots` has ONE `risk_score` column and NO session-risk/trajectory columns. The weekly-snapshot cron (T15) writes **roster** risk → `risk_score`; it must NOT compute `computeSessionRisk` at all (session risk is per-attempt/live, not weekly) and must NOT silently drop a computed value. **Trajectory** is derived on read from the snapshot history (the snapshots ARE the trajectory data) — not stored. So: T15 computes & writes roster risk only; **T16 (one-student read API) computes `computeSessionRisk` live from the attempt's `quiz_responses` telemetry AND derives trajectory from the student's snapshot history.** Remove the void-suppressed session-risk/trajectory writes from T15. (No new snapshot columns needed.)

- **P3-C4 — `diagnose()` call site must match the producer's signature (Tasks 14 → 16).** Task 14 (producer, Slice E) defines `DiagnoseInput = { divergence_score: number; hw_avg: number|null; quiz_avg: number|null; error_types: string[] }`. The Task 16 roster-signals route was drafted calling `diagnose({ hwAvg, quizAvg, divergencePts, avgHints, errorTypes })` — **wrong shape.** The call site MUST use Task 14's `DiagnoseInput` exactly (`divergence_score`, `hw_avg`, `quiz_avg`, `error_types`). Whoever implements T16 imports the `DiagnoseInput` type from `@/lib/signals/diagnosis` and conforms to it.

- **P3-C5 — Single source for the taxonomy seed (Tasks 1 ↔ 13).** The 14 `misconception_types` rows (8 `error_type` + 6 `reasoning_pattern` + display labels) are authored in BOTH `0011_signals.sql` (the `INSERT … ON CONFLICT DO NOTHING` seed, T1) and `src/lib/misconceptions/taxonomy.ts` (`MISCONCEPTION_TYPE_ROWS`, T13). These MUST be byte-identical (same codes, same `display_label`, same `kind`, same `sort_order`). T13's `taxonomy.ts` is the canonical source; when T1's migration is implemented (or re-checked at T17), reconcile its seed `display_label`/`sort_order` values against `taxonomy.ts`. Add a test (in T13 or T1) asserting the two lists match if cheap.

- **P3-C6 — `computeTrajectory` direction polarity (Tasks 9 → 15/16).** `computeTrajectory(history, lowerIsBetter=false)` defaults `lowerIsBetter=true` (V1 `computeTrend`). For **quiz-score** trajectories (higher is better), callers (T15 snapshot, T16 read) MUST pass `lowerIsBetter=false`, else "improving" and "worsening" invert. The producer returns `{ trajectory }`; call sites read `.trajectory`.

- **P3-C7 — `vitest` `beforeEach` import (Tasks 12, others).** Tests that reset a module-scope counter in `beforeEach` must `import { beforeEach } from 'vitest'` explicitly (this repo does not enable vitest globals). Match the existing engine test files' import style.

### Round-1 Codex corrections (P3-C8…C18 — apply WITH the above; these GOVERN over the task bodies)

- **P3-C8 — Teacher read routes need a STAFF role gate (Task 16).** `guardStudentAccess` allows the student themselves AND their parent; `guardClassAccess` is class-scoped, not role-scoped. The `/teacher/student/[id]/signals` and `/teacher/class/[id]/roster-signals` routes serve teacher-only data (`skill_learning_state`, `misconception_observations`) — a student/parent calling them would pass the object guard and leak that data. Gate on role FIRST: the caller's `get_my_role()` (or the existing role helper in `src/lib/auth/roles.ts`) must be `teacher|school_admin|school_sysadmin|platform_admin`, else 403. The `/api/teacher/` path prefix is NOT an authorization control.
- **P3-C9 — `0011` MUST tighten the `skill_learning_state` RLS and role-gate the misconception RLS (Tasks 1, 13).** The Foundation's `0005` `sls_school_read` is `USING (school_id = public.get_my_school_id() OR public.is_platform_admin())` — that lets ANY same-school authenticated user, **including students and parents**, read `skill_learning_state` (a live hole; the comment says "staff" but the policy doesn't enforce it). In `0011`: `DROP POLICY IF EXISTS sls_school_read` and recreate it STAFF-only: `USING ((public.get_my_role() IN ('teacher','school_admin','school_sysadmin','platform_admin') AND school_id = public.get_my_school_id()) OR public.is_platform_admin())`. Use the **same** staff-only shape for `misconception_observations`' read policy — do NOT ship the school-scope-only version (it repeats the hole). `get_my_role()` exists (0001).
- **P3-C10 — Task 6 recompute reads PHANTOM columns/tables — map `SkillStateInput` from REAL columns only.** It referenced `homework_attempts.grade` (use `score_pct` / `teacher_score`), `assignments.reteach_completed_at` (does not exist — derive a reteach event from the `0011` redo flags `homework_attempts.allow_redo/is_redo` + a graded redo, or omit the `reteach` input until a real field exists; `computeSkillState` accepts `reteach=null`), and `cognitive_signals` (no such table — derive `sessionErrorPatterns` from `quiz_responses.grading_output->>'reasoning_pattern'` and/or `misconception_observations`). Verify every column read against `supabase/migrations/*` before lifting.
- **P3-C11 — `recomputeSkillStatesForStudent` signature is the OBJECT form (Tasks 6 → 15).** Producer: `recomputeSkillStatesForStudent(admin, { studentId, schoolId, skillIds? })`. The Task 15 cron call `recomputeSkillStatesForStudent(admin, student_id, { classId })` is WRONG. Every call site uses the object arg; pass `schoolId` derived from `users.school_id` for the student (it is written to `skill_learning_state.school_id` at upsert).
- **P3-C12 — `computeRosterRiskIndex` takes RAW attempt arrays, not pre-aggregates (Tasks 10 → 15, 16).** Producer input: `{ homeworkAttempts: {score,submitted_at,allow_redo,is_redo}[]; quizAttempts: {score,submitted_at}[]; totalAssigned: number }`. The cron/read call sites drafted with `{ avgHwScore, avgQuizScore, completionRate, … }` are WRONG — fetch the raw attempt rows and pass them; the function computes its own averages/trend/recency internally.
- **P3-C13 — Session risk must neutralize ALL-ZERO telemetry, not just empty arrays (Task 11).** With zero sub-scores the verbatim ensemble still returns ≈0.135 (velocity-stable 0.3×0.2 + calibration 0.5×0.1 + engagement 0.5×0.05). Until the Plan-4 quiz UI captures telemetry, rows are all-zero — that must read as **no risk**, not 0.135. Add a guard: if every telemetry field across all responses is zero/absent, return `{ score: 0, factors: [] }` (or a flagged `'insufficient_telemetry'`), bypassing the ensemble. The ensemble + its weights stay verbatim for the real-data path.
- **P3-C14 — Read-API queries must SELECT the columns the producers consume (Task 16).** The one-student route uses `latestAttemptId` → must `select('id', …)` on `quiz_attempts`; `computeSessionRisk` needs the telemetry columns AND `is_correct` → `select('is_correct', 'response_time_ms', 'hesitation_ms', 'answer_changes', 'navigation_backs', 'pause_count', 'total_pause_ms', 'word_count', …)` on `quiz_responses`. Audit each producer's required fields and include them in every select (no missing-column `undefined`s feeding the math).
- **P3-C15 — `improvement_4w` is an EXACT 28-day lookup (Task 15).** Use `.eq('snapshot_date', priorMondayStr).maybeSingle()` where `priorMondayStr = snapshot_date − 28d`, NOT `.lte(...)` + newest-earlier-row. `NULL` if that exact prior row is absent.
- **P3-C16 — `effort_label` CHECK idempotency (Task 1).** `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS effort_label text CHECK(...)` does NOT add the CHECK if the column already exists without it. Split: `ADD COLUMN IF NOT EXISTS effort_label text;` then a DO-block drop-if-exists + `ADD CONSTRAINT homework_attempts_effort_label_check CHECK (effort_label IS NULL OR effort_label IN ('effortful_success','struggling_trying','independent_success','independent_struggle'))` — same idempotent pattern as the `grading_status`/`question_type` swaps.
- **P3-C17 — `misconception_types` must not be client-writable (Task 1).** Do NOT `GRANT ALL … TO authenticated, anon`. Grant `SELECT` to `authenticated, anon` and `ALL` only to `service_role` (the taxonomy reference vocabulary is read-only to clients). `misconception_observations` uses the staff-only read policy from P3-C9 + service-role writes.
- **P3-C18 — reteach effectiveness has no `homework_attempts.class_id` (Task 12).** `homework_attempts` has no `class_id` (class is via `assignments.class_id`). The pure `detectCompletedReteachCycles` input must use only columns that exist on `homework_attempts` (+ `assignment_id`); if class scoping is needed, the calling route joins `assignments` and maps `class_id` at the boundary — never read `homework_attempts.class_id`.
- **P3-C2 (extended) — Task 13 also reads phantom `quizzes(school_id)`.** Besides the composite-`responseId` fix, Task 13's `recordMisconceptions` wiring selects `quizzes(school_id)` which does NOT exist. Derive `school_id` via `quizzes.class_id → classes.school_id` (or the teacher's `users.school_id`), same as P3-C1.

### Round-2 Codex corrections (P3-C19…C21 + C13 reinforcement — apply WITH the above; these GOVERN over the task bodies)

- **P3-C19 — `sessionErrorPatterns` vocabulary MAPPING + source (Task 6).** `computeSkillState` expects `sessionErrorPatterns` in V1's session vocabulary (`conceptual` | `procedural` | `careless` | `random`) — these drive `conceptualShare`/`slipShare`, which gate NDI test 1 and `ready_to_extend`. The OEQ grader emits a DIFFERENT vocabulary (`error_type`, `reasoning_pattern`). If recompute feeds raw `reasoning_pattern` values, conceptual/slip shares are ALWAYS 0 and NDI test 1 never fires. Add a pure helper `src/lib/skills/errorPatternMap.ts` mapping graded-OEQ `grading_output` → the session vocabulary, applied in recompute before `computeSkillState`. Mapping (V2 derivation, recalibratable; unit-test it): `reasoning_pattern='misconception'`→`conceptual`; `error_type='reasoning_gap'`→`conceptual`; `error_type='vocabulary_confusion'`→`conceptual`; `reasoning_pattern='surface_recall'`→`procedural`; `error_type='incomplete'`→`procedural`; `error_type='factual_error'`→`careless`; `error_type='misunderstood_question'`→`careless`; `off_topic`/`blank`/`blank_or_off_topic`→`random`; `error_type='none'` or `reasoning_pattern∈{full_reasoning,creative_extension}`→omit. **Source rule (resolves round-2 #5):** `sessionErrorPatterns` derive ONLY from graded-OEQ `grading_output` via this map; `misconception_observations` is the recurring-error *feature* store for `findRecurringError`, NOT the session-pattern source.
- **P3-C20 — OEQ correctness for per-skill quiz observations (Task 6).** OEQ responses persist `ai_score` (0/0.5/1.0) but NOT `is_correct` (the submit route sets `is_correct` only for MCQ/numeric, positions 1-3 — verified `submit/route.ts:111-114` vs OEQ persist `:219-223`). Task 6's quiz-observation gather MUST NOT filter `.not('is_correct','is',null)` (it drops every OEQ). Derive the `SkillStateInput.quiz[].correct` boolean per question: MCQ/numeric → `is_correct`; OEQ → `(ai_score ?? 0) >= 0.5` (partial-or-better counts; V2 derivation, recalibratable). Gather BOTH question types (joined to `quiz_questions.skill_id`) so per-skill cold-accuracy reflects OEQ evidence.
- **P3-C21 — `0011` also tightens `student_model_snapshots` RLS (Task 1).** `0006`'s `sms_scoped_read` is `USING (student_id = auth.uid() OR school_id = public.get_my_school_id() OR is_platform_admin())` — the `school_id` clause lets ANY same-school authenticated user (incl. students/parents) read PEERS' snapshots (mastery_band/risk/strengths/struggles = peer-data leak). In `0011`: `DROP POLICY IF EXISTS "sms_scoped_read"` and recreate so students/parents read ONLY their own row (`student_id = auth.uid()`; add the guardian link for parents if modeled), STAFF read same-school (`public.get_my_role() IN ('teacher','school_admin','school_sysadmin','platform_admin') AND school_id = public.get_my_school_id()`), platform admin always. The student-growth API (T16) then returns only the caller's own snapshots.
- **P3-C13 (reinforced) — change the Task 11 TEST, not just the impl.** The drafted Task 11 test expects `computeSessionRisk([])` → `0.135`. Per P3-C13, BOTH empty AND all-zero telemetry must return `{ score: 0, factors: [] }`: change that assertion to expect `0` (not `0.135`) and ADD an all-zero-rows test asserting `score === 0`. The verbatim ensemble (with its `0.135` baseline) applies only to the real-telemetry path.

### Round-3 Codex corrections (P3-C22…C24 — apply WITH the above; these GOVERN over the task bodies)

- **P3-C22 — Task 15 must upsert `consistency_score` (not just `consistency_label`).** `0011` adds `student_model_snapshots.consistency_score` and `computeConsistency()` returns it, but the drafted cron upsert writes only `consistency_label`, leaving the new column permanently null. The snapshot upsert MUST include `consistency_score: consistencyResult.consistency_score`.
- **P3-C23 — Task 15 must write snapshot `mastery_band` by COPYING the quiz-band (NOT recomputing it).** `student_model_snapshots.mastery_band` exists (0006) and the student-growth API reads it, but the drafted cron never writes it. The cron MUST select the student's quiz rows (`mastery_band, submitted_at, created_at, is_complete`) and write `currentMasteryBand(quizRows)` (from `scoring.ts`) into the snapshot. This does NOT violate the two-instrument invariant — it copies the existing quiz-score band; it must NOT be derived from `computeSkillState`.
- **P3-C24 — Snapshot determinism: inject the reference date into wall-clock signals (Tasks 10, 15).** `computeRosterRiskIndex`'s recency component uses `Date.now()` internally (verbatim V1), so re-running the same `snapshot_date` later changes `risk_score`. Add an optional `referenceDate?: Date` (or `nowMs?: number`) parameter to `computeRosterRiskIndex` (defaulting to `new Date()` for live reads) and have the weekly-snapshot cron pass the canonical `snapshot_date`'s reference. Freeze the clock to `ref_date` in the cron tests. This is a justified V2 deviation from the byte-verbatim lift (the weekly snapshot must be re-runnable to the same values). Apply the same `referenceDate` injection to any other signal that reads a wall clock for recency/trend.
